tbm_grant_air_cas_kaiserreich = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1922_kaiserreich = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1936 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1936_kaiserreich = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1940 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1940_kaiserreich = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1944 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            tbm_grant_air_cas_y1944_kaiserreich = yes
        }
    }
}

tbm_grant_air_cas_y1922_kaiserreich = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = early_bombs }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_air value = 1922 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_air_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_cas
                has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
            }
            set_technology = { early_bombs = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}

                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }

            tbm_grant_land_infantry_y1944_kaiserreich = yes
        }
    }
}

                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_naval_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_submarines
                NOT = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
            }
            set_technology = { advanced_submarine = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_kaiserreich = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}
